import AppIntents
import OSLog
import SwiftUI
import UIKit
import WidgetKit

private let widgetLogger = Logger(
    subsystem: "com.raver.mvp.widget.selected-event-countdown",
    category: "SelectedEventCountdownWidget"
)

private func debugWidgetLog(_ message: String) {
    widgetLogger.debug("\(message, privacy: .public)")
    print("[SelectedEventCountdownWidget] \(message)")
    WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[SelectedEventCountdownWidget] \(message)")
}

private func errorWidgetLog(_ message: String) {
    widgetLogger.error("\(message, privacy: .public)")
    print("[SelectedEventCountdownWidget][error] \(message)")
    WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[SelectedEventCountdownWidget][error] \(message)")
}

struct WidgetEventIDOptionsProvider: DynamicOptionsProvider {
    func results() async throws -> IntentItemCollection<String> {
        let snapshot = try WidgetSelectableEventsStore.shared.loadSnapshot()
        debugWidgetLog("event options snapshotCount=\(snapshot.events.count)")
        let items = snapshot.events.map { event in
            debugWidgetLog("event option id=\(event.id) cover=\(event.coverImageURL ?? "nil") lineup=\(event.lineupImageURL ?? "nil") preferred=\(event.preferredBackgroundURL ?? "nil")")

            let subtitleText = [event.city, event.venueName]
                .compactMap { value -> String? in
                    let trimmed = value?.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines) ?? ""
                    return trimmed.isEmpty ? nil : trimmed
                }
                .joined(separator: " · ")

            return IntentItem(
                event.id,
                title: LocalizedStringResource(stringLiteral: event.name),
                subtitle: subtitleText.isEmpty ? nil : LocalizedStringResource(stringLiteral: subtitleText)
            )
        }

        return IntentItemCollection(
            promptLabel: "选择一个活动",
            sections: [
                IntentItemSection(items: items)
            ]
        )
    }
}

struct SelectedEventCountdownConfigurationIntent: WidgetConfigurationIntent {
    static var title: LocalizedStringResource = "Selected Event Countdown"
    static var description = IntentDescription("Pick an event to pin as a countdown widget.")

    @Parameter(title: "Event", optionsProvider: WidgetEventIDOptionsProvider())
    var eventID: String?
}

struct SelectedEventCountdownEntry: TimelineEntry {
    enum ContentState {
        case unconfigured
        case missing
        case upcoming(event: WidgetSelectableEvent, remainingDays: Int)
        case ongoing(event: WidgetSelectableEvent, startedDaysAgo: Int)
        case ended(event: WidgetSelectableEvent, endedDaysAgo: Int)
    }

    let date: Date
    let configuration: SelectedEventCountdownConfigurationIntent
    let state: ContentState
}

struct SelectedEventCountdownProvider: AppIntentTimelineProvider {
    func placeholder(in context: Context) -> SelectedEventCountdownEntry {
        debugWidgetLog("placeholder entry requested")
        return sampleEntry()
    }

    func snapshot(
        for configuration: SelectedEventCountdownConfigurationIntent,
        in context: Context
    ) async -> SelectedEventCountdownEntry {
        debugWidgetLog("snapshot requested preview=\(context.isPreview) selectedID=\(configuration.eventID ?? "nil")")
        if context.isPreview, configuration.eventID == nil {
            return sampleEntry(configuration: configuration)
        }
        return entry(for: configuration, now: Date())
    }

    func timeline(
        for configuration: SelectedEventCountdownConfigurationIntent,
        in context: Context
    ) async -> Timeline<SelectedEventCountdownEntry> {
        let now = Date()
        let entry = entry(for: configuration, now: now)
        let policy = TimelineReloadPolicy.after(nextRefreshDate(for: entry, now: now))
        return Timeline(entries: [entry], policy: policy)
    }

    private func entry(
        for configuration: SelectedEventCountdownConfigurationIntent,
        now: Date
    ) -> SelectedEventCountdownEntry {
        guard let selectedID = configuration.eventID else {
            debugWidgetLog("entry state=unconfigured")
            return SelectedEventCountdownEntry(
                date: now,
                configuration: configuration,
                state: .unconfigured
            )
        }

        guard
            let snapshot = try? WidgetSelectableEventsStore.shared.loadSnapshot(),
            let event = snapshot.events.first(where: { $0.id == selectedID }),
            let startDate = event.startDate,
            let endDate = event.endDate
        else {
            errorWidgetLog("entry state=missing selectedID=\(selectedID)")
            return SelectedEventCountdownEntry(
                date: now,
                configuration: configuration,
                state: .missing
            )
        }

        debugWidgetLog("entry selected id=\(event.id) cover=\(event.coverImageURL ?? "nil") lineup=\(event.lineupImageURL ?? "nil") preferred=\(event.preferredBackgroundURL ?? "nil")")

        if now < startDate {
            let remainingDays = Calendar.current.dateComponents(
                [.day],
                from: Calendar.current.startOfDay(for: now),
                to: Calendar.current.startOfDay(for: startDate)
            ).day ?? 0

            debugWidgetLog("entry state=upcoming id=\(event.id) remainingDays=\(max(0, remainingDays))")
            return SelectedEventCountdownEntry(
                date: now,
                configuration: configuration,
                state: .upcoming(event: event, remainingDays: max(0, remainingDays))
            )
        }

        if now <= endDate {
            let startedDaysAgo = Calendar.current.dateComponents(
                [.day],
                from: Calendar.current.startOfDay(for: startDate),
                to: Calendar.current.startOfDay(for: now)
            ).day ?? 0

            debugWidgetLog("entry state=ongoing id=\(event.id) startedDaysAgo=\(max(0, startedDaysAgo))")
            return SelectedEventCountdownEntry(
                date: now,
                configuration: configuration,
                state: .ongoing(event: event, startedDaysAgo: max(0, startedDaysAgo))
            )
        }

        let endedDaysAgo = Calendar.current.dateComponents(
            [.day],
            from: Calendar.current.startOfDay(for: endDate),
            to: Calendar.current.startOfDay(for: now)
        ).day ?? 0

        debugWidgetLog("entry state=ended id=\(event.id) endedDaysAgo=\(max(0, endedDaysAgo))")
        return SelectedEventCountdownEntry(
            date: now,
            configuration: configuration,
            state: .ended(event: event, endedDaysAgo: max(0, endedDaysAgo))
        )
    }

    private func nextRefreshDate(for entry: SelectedEventCountdownEntry, now: Date) -> Date {
        switch entry.state {
        case .unconfigured, .missing:
            return Calendar.current.date(byAdding: .minute, value: 5, to: now) ?? now.addingTimeInterval(5 * 60)
        case .ongoing(let event, _):
            guard let endDate = event.endDate else {
                return Calendar.current.date(byAdding: .hour, value: 1, to: now) ?? now.addingTimeInterval(3600)
            }
            let nextCheckpoint = Calendar.current.nextDate(
                after: now,
                matching: DateComponents(hour: 0, minute: 5),
                matchingPolicy: .nextTime
            ) ?? now.addingTimeInterval(24 * 3600)
            let eventTransition = min(endDate.addingTimeInterval(60), nextCheckpoint)
            return eventTransition > now ? eventTransition : nextCheckpoint
        case .upcoming(let event, _):
            guard let startDate = event.startDate else {
                return Calendar.current.date(byAdding: .hour, value: 1, to: now) ?? now.addingTimeInterval(3600)
            }
            let nextCheckpoint = Calendar.current.nextDate(
                after: now,
                matching: DateComponents(hour: 0, minute: 5),
                matchingPolicy: .nextTime
            ) ?? now.addingTimeInterval(24 * 3600)
            let eventTransition = min(startDate.addingTimeInterval(60), nextCheckpoint)
            return eventTransition > now ? eventTransition : nextCheckpoint
        case .ended:
            return Calendar.current.date(byAdding: .hour, value: 12, to: now) ?? now.addingTimeInterval(12 * 3600)
        }
    }

    private func sampleEntry(
        configuration: SelectedEventCountdownConfigurationIntent = SelectedEventCountdownConfigurationIntent()
    ) -> SelectedEventCountdownEntry {
        debugWidgetLog("sample entry used selectedID=\(configuration.eventID ?? "nil")")

        return SelectedEventCountdownEntry(
            date: Date(),
            configuration: configuration,
            state: .unconfigured
        )
    }
}

struct SelectedEventCountdownWidgetEntryView: View {
    @Environment(\.widgetFamily) private var family

    let entry: SelectedEventCountdownEntry

    private var isUsingCachedBackground: Bool {
        guard let currentEvent else { return false }
        return WidgetBackgroundImageCache.loadImageData(relativePath: currentEvent.cachedBackgroundImageRelativePath) != nil
    }

    var body: some View {
        ZStack {
            backgroundLayer
            overlayLayer
            contentLayer
            debugBadge
        }
        .widgetURL(widgetURL)
        .containerBackground(for: .widget) {
            Color.black
        }
        .unredacted()
    }

    @ViewBuilder
    private var backgroundLayer: some View {
        if let currentEvent,
           let cachedData = WidgetBackgroundImageCache.loadImageData(relativePath: currentEvent.cachedBackgroundImageRelativePath),
           let image = UIImage(data: cachedData) {
            let _ = Self.debugLogCachedBackground(eventID: currentEvent.id, relativePath: currentEvent.cachedBackgroundImageRelativePath)
            Image(uiImage: image)
                .resizable()
                .scaledToFill()
                .frame(maxWidth: .infinity, maxHeight: .infinity)
                .clipped()
        } else if let imageURL = currentEvent?.preferredBackgroundURL, let url = URL(string: imageURL) {
            let _ = Self.debugLogBackgroundURL(imageURL)
            WidgetRemoteBackgroundImage(
                url: url,
                sourceLabel: currentEvent?.id ?? "unknown"
            ) {
                gradientBackground
            }
        } else {
            let _ = Self.debugLogNoBackgroundURL(currentEvent?.id)
            gradientBackground
        }
    }

    private var overlayLayer: some View {
        LinearGradient(
            colors: [
                Color.black.opacity(0.18),
                Color.black.opacity(0.48),
                Color.black.opacity(0.82)
            ],
            startPoint: .top,
            endPoint: .bottom
        )
    }

    @ViewBuilder
    private var debugBadge: some View {
        VStack {
            HStack {
                Text(debugBadgeText)
                    .font(.caption2.monospaced().weight(.bold))
                    .foregroundStyle(.white)
                    .padding(.horizontal, 8)
                    .padding(.vertical, 5)
                    .background(Color.black.opacity(0.58), in: Capsule())
                Spacer()
            }
            Spacer()
        }
        .padding(10)
        .allowsHitTesting(false)
    }

    @ViewBuilder
    private var contentLayer: some View {
        switch entry.state {
        case .unconfigured:
            statusLayout(
                title: "还未选择活动",
                subtitle: "长按组件后选择一个活动"
            )
        case .missing:
            statusLayout(
                title: "活动数据不可用",
                subtitle: "请重新选择倒计时活动"
            )
        case .upcoming(let event, let remainingDays):
            countdownLayout(event: event, remainingDays: remainingDays)
        case .ongoing(let event, let startedDaysAgo):
            eventStatusLayout(
                event: event,
                headline: startedDaysAgo == 0 ? "今天正在进行" : "已经开始 \(startedDaysAgo) 天"
            )
        case .ended(let event, let endedDaysAgo):
            eventStatusLayout(
                event: event,
                headline: "已经结束 \(endedDaysAgo) 天"
            )
        }
    }

    private func countdownLayout(event: WidgetSelectableEvent, remainingDays: Int) -> some View {
        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: family == .systemSmall ? 8 : 10) {
            Spacer()

            if family == .systemMedium {
                if let meta = eventMetaText(event) {
                    Text(meta)
                        .font(.caption2.weight(.medium))
                        .foregroundStyle(Color.white.opacity(0.78))
                        .lineLimit(1)
                }
            }

            Text(event.name)
                .font(family == .systemSmall ? .headline.weight(.bold) : .title3.weight(.bold))
                .foregroundStyle(.white)
                .lineLimit(2)

            if family == .systemSmall {
                Text("还有 \(remainingDays) 天")
                    .font(.title2.weight(.heavy))
                    .foregroundStyle(.white)
            } else {
                Text("距离 \(event.name) 还有 \(remainingDays) 天")
                    .font(.subheadline.weight(.semibold))
                    .foregroundStyle(.white.opacity(0.96))
                    .lineLimit(2)
            }
        }
        .frame(maxWidth: .infinity, maxHeight: .infinity, alignment: .bottomLeading)
        .padding(family == .systemSmall ? 14 : 16)
    }

    private func statusLayout(title: String, subtitle: String) -> some View {
        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 8) {
            Spacer()
            Text(title)
                .font(family == .systemSmall ? .headline.weight(.bold) : .title3.weight(.bold))
                .foregroundStyle(.white)
                .lineLimit(2)
            Text(subtitle)
                .font(.caption.weight(.medium))
                .foregroundStyle(Color.white.opacity(0.82))
                .lineLimit(3)
        }
        .frame(maxWidth: .infinity, maxHeight: .infinity, alignment: .bottomLeading)
        .padding(family == .systemSmall ? 14 : 16)
    }

    private func eventStatusLayout(event: WidgetSelectableEvent, headline: String) -> some View {
        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: family == .systemSmall ? 8 : 10) {
            Spacer()

            if family == .systemMedium, let meta = eventMetaText(event) {
                Text(meta)
                    .font(.caption2.weight(.medium))
                    .foregroundStyle(Color.white.opacity(0.78))
                    .lineLimit(1)
            }

            Text(event.name)
                .font(family == .systemSmall ? .headline.weight(.bold) : .title3.weight(.bold))
                .foregroundStyle(.white)
                .lineLimit(2)

            Text(headline)
                .font(family == .systemSmall ? .title3.weight(.heavy) : .subheadline.weight(.semibold))
                .foregroundStyle(.white.opacity(0.96))
                .lineLimit(2)
        }
        .frame(maxWidth: .infinity, maxHeight: .infinity, alignment: .bottomLeading)
        .padding(family == .systemSmall ? 14 : 16)
    }

    private var gradientBackground: some View {
        LinearGradient(
            colors: [
                Color(red: 0.16, green: 0.17, blue: 0.28),
                Color(red: 0.29, green: 0.17, blue: 0.47),
                Color(red: 0.07, green: 0.08, blue: 0.12)
            ],
            startPoint: .topLeading,
            endPoint: .bottomTrailing
        )
    }

    private var currentEvent: WidgetSelectableEvent? {
        switch entry.state {
        case .ongoing(let event, _):
            return event
        case .ended(let event, _):
            return event
        case .upcoming(let event, _):
            return event
        case .unconfigured, .missing:
            return nil
        }
    }

    private var debugBadgeText: String {
        let stateLabel: String
        switch entry.state {
        case .unconfigured:
            stateLabel = "unconfigured"
        case .missing:
            stateLabel = "missing"
        case .ongoing:
            stateLabel = "ongoing"
        case .ended:
            stateLabel = "ended"
        case .upcoming:
            stateLabel = "upcoming"
        }

        let suffix = currentEvent.map { String($0.id.suffix(6)) } ?? "none"
        return "\(stateLabel) · \(suffix)"
    }

    private var widgetURL: URL? {
        switch entry.state {
        case .upcoming(let event, _), .ongoing(let event, _), .ended(let event, _):
            return URL(string: event.deeplinkURL)
        case .unconfigured, .missing:
            return URL(string: "raver://")
        }
    }

    private func eventMetaText(_ event: WidgetSelectableEvent) -> String? {
        let parts = [event.city, event.venueName]
            .compactMap { value -> String? in
                let trimmed = value?.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines) ?? ""
                return trimmed.isEmpty ? nil : trimmed
            }
        guard !parts.isEmpty else { return nil }
        return parts.joined(separator: " · ")
    }

    private static func debugLogBackgroundURL(_ url: String) {
        debugWidgetLog("render background url=\(url)")
    }

    private static func debugLogCachedBackground(eventID: String, relativePath: String?) {
        debugWidgetLog("render cached background eventID=\(eventID) relativePath=\(relativePath ?? "nil")")
    }

    private static func debugLogNoBackgroundURL(_ eventID: String?) {
        errorWidgetLog("render no background url eventID=\(eventID ?? "nil")")
    }
}

private struct WidgetRemoteBackgroundImage<Fallback: View>: View {
    let url: URL
    let sourceLabel: String
    @ViewBuilder var fallback: () -> Fallback

    @State private var loadedImage: UIImage?

    var body: some View {
        Group {
            if let loadedImage {
                Image(uiImage: loadedImage)
                    .resizable()
                    .scaledToFill()
            } else {
                fallback()
            }
        }
        .task(id: url.absoluteString) {
            await load()
        }
    }

    @Sendable
    private func load() async {
        do {
            let request = URLRequest(
                url: url,
                cachePolicy: .reloadIgnoringLocalCacheData,
                timeoutInterval: 20
            )
            debugWidgetLog(
                "image request start source=\(sourceLabel) scheme=\(url.scheme ?? "nil") host=\(url.host ?? "nil") path=\(url.path) absolute=\(url.absoluteString)"
            )

            let (data, response) = try await URLSession.shared.data(for: request)
            let statusCode = (response as? HTTPURLResponse)?.statusCode ?? -1
            debugWidgetLog("image request response source=\(sourceLabel) status=\(statusCode) bytes=\(data.count)")

            guard statusCode == -1 || (200...299).contains(statusCode) else {
                errorWidgetLog("image request non-success source=\(sourceLabel) status=\(statusCode) url=\(url.absoluteString)")
                return
            }

            guard let image = UIImage(data: data) else {
                errorWidgetLog("image decode failed source=\(sourceLabel) bytes=\(data.count) url=\(url.absoluteString)")
                return
            }

            let renderedImage = centerCroppedSquareImage(from: image)

            await MainActor.run {
                loadedImage = renderedImage
            }
            debugWidgetLog("image request success source=\(sourceLabel) size=\(Int(renderedImage.size.width))x\(Int(renderedImage.size.height))")
        } catch {
            errorWidgetLog("image request failed source=\(sourceLabel) url=\(url.absoluteString) error=\(error.localizedDescription)")
        }
    }

    private func centerCroppedSquareImage(from image: UIImage) -> UIImage {
        guard let cgImage = image.cgImage else { return image }

        let width = CGFloat(cgImage.width)
        let height = CGFloat(cgImage.height)
        let edge = min(width, height)
        let cropRect = CGRect(
            x: (width - edge) * 0.5,
            y: (height - edge) * 0.5,
            width: edge,
            height: edge
        ).integral

        guard let croppedCGImage = cgImage.cropping(to: cropRect) else {
            return image
        }

        return UIImage(
            cgImage: croppedCGImage,
            scale: image.scale,
            orientation: image.imageOrientation
        )
    }
}

struct RaverSelectedEventCountdownWidget: Widget {
    let kind: String = "RaverSelectedEventCountdownWidgetV4"

    var body: some WidgetConfiguration {
        AppIntentConfiguration(
            kind: kind,
            intent: SelectedEventCountdownConfigurationIntent.self,
            provider: SelectedEventCountdownProvider()
        ) { entry in
            SelectedEventCountdownWidgetEntryView(entry: entry)
        }
        .contentMarginsDisabled()
        .configurationDisplayName("活动倒计时")
        .description("手动选择一个活动，把它固定在桌面上倒计时。")
        .supportedFamilies([.systemSmall, .systemMedium])
    }
}

@main
struct RaverSelectedEventCountdownWidgetBundle: WidgetBundle {
    var body: some Widget {
        RaverSelectedEventCountdownWidget()
    }
}

import Foundation

#if canImport(UIKit)
import UIKit
#endif

enum WidgetSharedConstants {
    static let appGroupIdentifier = "group.com.raver.mvp"
    static let selectableEventsFileName = "widget-selectable-events.json"
    static let debugLogFileName = "widget-debug.log"
    static let cachedImagesDirectoryName = "widget-event-images"
}

enum WidgetSharedDebugLog {
    static func append(_ message: String) {
        let formatted = "[\(timestamp())] \(message)\n"
        guard let data = formatted.data(using: .utf8) else { return }

        do {
            let fileManager = FileManager.default
            let url = try logFileURL(fileManager: fileManager)
            let directory = url.deletingLastPathComponent()
            if !fileManager.fileExists(atPath: directory.path) {
                try fileManager.createDirectory(at: directory, withIntermediateDirectories: true)
            }

            if !fileManager.fileExists(atPath: url.path) {
                try data.write(to: url, options: .atomic)
                return
            }

            let handle = try FileHandle(forWritingTo: url)
            defer { try? handle.close() }
            try handle.seekToEnd()
            try handle.write(contentsOf: data)
        } catch {
            print("[WidgetSharedDebugLog][error] append failed: \(error.localizedDescription)")
        }
    }

    static func clear() {
        do {
            let fileManager = FileManager.default
            let url = try logFileURL(fileManager: fileManager)
            if fileManager.fileExists(atPath: url.path) {
                try fileManager.removeItem(at: url)
            }
        } catch {
            print("[WidgetSharedDebugLog][error] clear failed: \(error.localizedDescription)")
        }
    }

    private static func logFileURL(fileManager: FileManager) throws -> URL {
        if let container = fileManager.containerURL(
            forSecurityApplicationGroupIdentifier: WidgetSharedConstants.appGroupIdentifier
        ) {
            return container.appendingPathComponent(WidgetSharedConstants.debugLogFileName, isDirectory: false)
        }

        let applicationSupport = try fileManager.url(
            for: .applicationSupportDirectory,
            in: .userDomainMask,
            appropriateFor: nil,
            create: true
        )
        return applicationSupport
            .appendingPathComponent("WidgetFallback", isDirectory: true)
            .appendingPathComponent(WidgetSharedConstants.debugLogFileName, isDirectory: false)
    }

    private static func timestamp() -> String {
        WidgetSelectableEvent.iso8601Formatter.string(from: Date())
    }
}

struct WidgetSelectableEvent: Codable, Identifiable, Hashable {
    let id: String
    let name: String
    let startDateISO8601: String
    let endDateISO8601: String?
    let coverImageURL: String?
    let lineupImageURL: String?
    let city: String?
    let venueName: String?
    let deeplinkURL: String
    let addedAtISO8601: String
    let cachedBackgroundImageRelativePath: String?
    let cachedBackgroundImageSourceURL: String?
}

struct WidgetSelectableEventsSnapshot: Codable, Hashable {
    let version: Int
    let generatedAtISO8601: String
    let events: [WidgetSelectableEvent]
}

extension WidgetSelectableEvent {
    var startDate: Date? {
        Self.iso8601Formatter.date(from: startDateISO8601)
    }

    var endDate: Date? {
        guard let endDateISO8601 else { return nil }
        return Self.iso8601Formatter.date(from: endDateISO8601)
    }

    var addedAt: Date? {
        Self.iso8601Formatter.date(from: addedAtISO8601)
    }

    var preferredBackgroundURL: String? {
        let cover = coverImageURL?.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
        if let cover, !cover.isEmpty {
            return cover
        }
        let lineup = lineupImageURL?.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
        if let lineup, !lineup.isEmpty {
            return lineup
        }
        return nil
    }

    static let iso8601Formatter: ISO8601DateFormatter = {
        let formatter = ISO8601DateFormatter()
        formatter.formatOptions = [.withInternetDateTime, .withFractionalSeconds]
        return formatter
    }()
}

enum WidgetBackgroundImageCache {
    private struct CachePayload {
        let data: Data
        let fileExtension: String
    }

    static func fetchAndStore(
        eventID: String,
        remoteURLString: String
    ) async -> String? {
        guard let remoteURL = URL(string: remoteURLString) else {
            WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache][error] invalid cache url eventID=\(eventID) remote=\(remoteURLString)")
            return nil
        }

        do {
            let directory = try sharedContainerRootURL()
                .appendingPathComponent(WidgetSharedConstants.cachedImagesDirectoryName, isDirectory: true)
            if !FileManager.default.fileExists(atPath: directory.path) {
                try FileManager.default.createDirectory(at: directory, withIntermediateDirectories: true)
            }

            WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache] cache fetch start eventID=\(eventID) url=\(remoteURLString)")
            let (data, response) = try await URLSession.shared.data(from: remoteURL)
            let statusCode = (response as? HTTPURLResponse)?.statusCode ?? -1
            guard statusCode == -1 || (200...299).contains(statusCode) else {
                WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache][error] cache fetch non-success eventID=\(eventID) status=\(statusCode)")
                return nil
            }

            let payload = cachePayload(from: remoteURLString, originalData: data) ?? CachePayload(
                data: data,
                fileExtension: widgetNonEmpty(remoteURL.pathExtension) ?? "img"
            )
            let finalURL = try sharedContainerRootURL()
                .appendingPathComponent(relativePath(eventID: eventID, fileExtension: payload.fileExtension), isDirectory: false)
            try payload.data.write(to: finalURL, options: .atomic)
            let relativePath = relativePath(eventID: eventID, fileExtension: payload.fileExtension)
            WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache] cache fetch success eventID=\(eventID) bytes=\(payload.data.count) relativePath=\(relativePath)")
            return relativePath
        } catch {
            WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache][error] cache fetch failed eventID=\(eventID) error=\(error.localizedDescription)")
            return nil
        }
    }

    static func loadImageData(relativePath: String?) -> Data? {
        guard let relativePath = widgetNonEmpty(relativePath) else { return nil }

        do {
            let url = try sharedContainerRootURL().appendingPathComponent(relativePath, isDirectory: false)
            guard FileManager.default.fileExists(atPath: url.path) else {
                WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache][error] cache miss relativePath=\(relativePath)")
                return nil
            }
            let data = try Data(contentsOf: url)
            WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache] cache load hit relativePath=\(relativePath) bytes=\(data.count)")
            return data
        } catch {
            WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache][error] cache load failed relativePath=\(relativePath) error=\(error.localizedDescription)")
            return nil
        }
    }

    static func remove(relativePath: String?) {
        guard let relativePath = widgetNonEmpty(relativePath) else { return }

        do {
            let url = try sharedContainerRootURL().appendingPathComponent(relativePath, isDirectory: false)
            guard FileManager.default.fileExists(atPath: url.path) else { return }
            try FileManager.default.removeItem(at: url)
            WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache] cache remove success relativePath=\(relativePath)")
        } catch {
            WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache][error] cache remove failed relativePath=\(relativePath) error=\(error.localizedDescription)")
        }
    }

    static func relativePath(eventID: String, fileExtension: String) -> String {
        return "\(WidgetSharedConstants.cachedImagesDirectoryName)/\(eventID).\(fileExtension)"
    }

    private static func cachedFileURL(eventID: String, fileExtension: String) -> URL? {
        do {
            return try sharedContainerRootURL()
                .appendingPathComponent(relativePath(eventID: eventID, fileExtension: fileExtension), isDirectory: false)
        } catch {
            WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetBackgroundImageCache][error] cache path build failed eventID=\(eventID) error=\(error.localizedDescription)")
            return nil
        }
    }

    private static func cachePayload(from remoteURLString: String, originalData: Data?) -> CachePayload? {
        guard let originalData else { return nil }

        if let processedData = centerCroppedSquareImageData(from: originalData) {
            return CachePayload(data: processedData, fileExtension: "jpg")
        }

        let fallbackExtension = widgetNonEmpty(URL(string: remoteURLString)?.pathExtension) ?? "img"
        return CachePayload(data: originalData, fileExtension: fallbackExtension)
    }

    private static func sharedContainerRootURL() throws -> URL {
        if let container = FileManager.default.containerURL(
            forSecurityApplicationGroupIdentifier: WidgetSharedConstants.appGroupIdentifier
        ) {
            return container
        }

        return try FileManager.default.url(
            for: .applicationSupportDirectory,
            in: .userDomainMask,
            appropriateFor: nil,
            create: true
        ).appendingPathComponent("WidgetFallback", isDirectory: true)
    }

    private static func centerCroppedSquareImageData(from data: Data) -> Data? {
        #if canImport(UIKit)
        guard let image = UIImage(data: data), let cgImage = image.cgImage else {
            return nil
        }

        let width = CGFloat(cgImage.width)
        let height = CGFloat(cgImage.height)
        let edge = min(width, height)
        let cropRect = CGRect(
            x: (width - edge) * 0.5,
            y: (height - edge) * 0.5,
            width: edge,
            height: edge
        ).integral

        guard let croppedCGImage = cgImage.cropping(to: cropRect) else {
            return nil
        }

        let croppedImage = UIImage(
            cgImage: croppedCGImage,
            scale: image.scale,
            orientation: image.imageOrientation
        )
        let normalizedImage = resizedSquareImageIfNeeded(croppedImage, maxEdge: 1200)
        return normalizedImage.jpegData(compressionQuality: 0.86)
        #else
        return nil
        #endif
    }

    private static func resizedSquareImageIfNeeded(_ image: UIImage, maxEdge: CGFloat) -> UIImage {
        let width = image.size.width
        let height = image.size.height
        let edge = min(width, height)
        guard edge > maxEdge, maxEdge > 0 else { return image }

        let targetSize = CGSize(width: maxEdge, height: maxEdge)
        let renderer = UIGraphicsImageRenderer(size: targetSize)
        return renderer.image { _ in
            image.draw(in: CGRect(origin: .zero, size: targetSize))
        }
    }
}

private func widgetNonEmpty(_ value: String?) -> String? {
    guard let value else { return nil }
    let trimmed = value.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
    return trimmed.isEmpty ? nil : trimmed
}

import Foundation

extension WidgetSelectableEvent {
    static func from(event: WebEvent, addedAt: Date = Date()) -> WidgetSelectableEvent {
        WidgetSelectableEvent(
            id: event.id,
            name: event.name,
            startDateISO8601: iso8601Formatter.string(from: event.startDate),
            endDateISO8601: iso8601Formatter.string(from: event.endDate),
            coverImageURL: AppConfig.resolvedURLString(event.coverAssetURL),
            lineupImageURL: AppConfig.resolvedURLString(event.lineupAssetURLs.first),
            city: event.city,
            venueName: normalizedWidgetVenueName(from: event),
            deeplinkURL: "raver://event/\(event.id)",
            addedAtISO8601: iso8601Formatter.string(from: addedAt),
            cachedBackgroundImageRelativePath: nil,
            cachedBackgroundImageSourceURL: nil
        )
    }

    private static func normalizedWidgetVenueName(from event: WebEvent) -> String? {
        let trimmed = event.summaryLocation.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
        return trimmed.isEmpty ? nil : trimmed
    }
}


===== FILE: /Users/blackie/Projects/raver/mobile/ios/RaverMVP/RaverMVP/Core/Widget/WidgetSelectableEventsStore.swift =====

import Foundation

final class WidgetSelectableEventsStore {
    static let shared = WidgetSelectableEventsStore()

    private let fileManager: FileManager
    private let encoder: JSONEncoder
    private let decoder: JSONDecoder
    private let iso8601Formatter: ISO8601DateFormatter

    init(fileManager: FileManager = .default) {
        self.fileManager = fileManager

        let encoder = JSONEncoder()
        encoder.outputFormatting = [.prettyPrinted, .sortedKeys]
        self.encoder = encoder

        self.decoder = JSONDecoder()

        let iso8601Formatter = ISO8601DateFormatter()
        iso8601Formatter.formatOptions = [.withInternetDateTime, .withFractionalSeconds]
        self.iso8601Formatter = iso8601Formatter
    }

    func loadSnapshot() throws -> WidgetSelectableEventsSnapshot {
        let url = try snapshotURL()
        guard fileManager.fileExists(atPath: url.path) else {
            return emptySnapshot()
        }
        let data = try Data(contentsOf: url)
        return try decoder.decode(WidgetSelectableEventsSnapshot.self, from: data)
    }

    @discardableResult
    func upsert(widgetEvent: WidgetSelectableEvent, generatedAt: Date = Date()) throws -> WidgetSelectableEvent {
        var snapshot = try loadSnapshot()

        if let index = snapshot.events.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == widgetEvent.id }) {
            var events = snapshot.events
            events[index] = widgetEvent
            snapshot = WidgetSelectableEventsSnapshot(
                version: snapshot.version,
                generatedAtISO8601: iso8601String(from: generatedAt),
                events: sort(events)
            )
        } else {
            snapshot = WidgetSelectableEventsSnapshot(
                version: snapshot.version,
                generatedAtISO8601: iso8601String(from: generatedAt),
                events: sort(snapshot.events + [widgetEvent])
            )
        }

        try persist(snapshot)
        return widgetEvent
    }

    @discardableResult
    func remove(eventID: String, generatedAt: Date = Date()) throws -> WidgetSelectableEvent? {
        var snapshot = try loadSnapshot()
        guard let index = snapshot.events.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == eventID }) else {
            return nil
        }

        var events = snapshot.events
        let removedEvent = events.remove(at: index)
        snapshot = WidgetSelectableEventsSnapshot(
            version: snapshot.version,
            generatedAtISO8601: iso8601String(from: generatedAt),
            events: sort(events)
        )
        try persist(snapshot)
        return removedEvent
    }

    func contains(eventID: String) -> Bool {
        (try? loadSnapshot().events.contains(where: { $0.id == eventID })) ?? false
    }

    private func persist(_ snapshot: WidgetSelectableEventsSnapshot) throws {
        let url = try snapshotURL()
        try ensureDirectoryExists(for: url.deletingLastPathComponent())
        let data = try encoder.encode(snapshot)
        try data.write(to: url, options: .atomic)
    }

    private func snapshotURL() throws -> URL {
        if let container = fileManager.containerURL(
            forSecurityApplicationGroupIdentifier: WidgetSharedConstants.appGroupIdentifier
        ) {
            return container.appendingPathComponent(WidgetSharedConstants.selectableEventsFileName, isDirectory: false)
        }

        let applicationSupport = try fileManager.url(
            for: .applicationSupportDirectory,
            in: .userDomainMask,
            appropriateFor: nil,
            create: true
        )
        return applicationSupport
            .appendingPathComponent("WidgetFallback", isDirectory: true)
            .appendingPathComponent(WidgetSharedConstants.selectableEventsFileName, isDirectory: false)
    }

    private func ensureDirectoryExists(for directoryURL: URL) throws {
        if !fileManager.fileExists(atPath: directoryURL.path) {
            try fileManager.createDirectory(at: directoryURL, withIntermediateDirectories: true, attributes: nil)
        }
    }

    private func emptySnapshot(now: Date = Date()) -> WidgetSelectableEventsSnapshot {
        WidgetSelectableEventsSnapshot(
            version: 1,
            generatedAtISO8601: iso8601String(from: now),
            events: []
        )
    }

    private func sort(_ events: [WidgetSelectableEvent]) -> [WidgetSelectableEvent] {
        events.sorted { lhs, rhs in
            let lhsDate = lhs.addedAt ?? .distantPast
            let rhsDate = rhs.addedAt ?? .distantPast
            if lhsDate != rhsDate {
                return lhsDate > rhsDate
            }
            return lhs.name.localizedCaseInsensitiveCompare(rhs.name) == .orderedAscending
        }
    }

    private func iso8601String(from date: Date) -> String {
        iso8601Formatter.string(from: date)
    }
}

import Foundation

extension WidgetSelectableEventsStore {
    @discardableResult
    func upsert(event: WebEvent, addedAt: Date = Date()) throws -> WidgetSelectableEvent {
        let widgetEvent = WidgetSelectableEvent.from(event: event, addedAt: addedAt)
        return try upsert(widgetEvent: widgetEvent, generatedAt: addedAt)
    }
}


===== FILE: /Users/blackie/Projects/raver/mobile/ios/RaverMVP/RaverMVP/Core/Widget/WidgetSelectableEventsSyncService.swift =====

import Foundation
import OSLog

#if canImport(WidgetKit)
import WidgetKit
#endif

enum WidgetSelectableEventAddResult {
    case added
    case refreshed
}

enum WidgetSelectableEventRemoveResult {
    case removed
    case notFound
}

final class WidgetSelectableEventsSyncService {
    static let shared = WidgetSelectableEventsSyncService()

    private static let logger = Logger(
        subsystem: Bundle.main.bundleIdentifier ?? "com.raver.mvp",
        category: "WidgetSelectableEventsSyncService"
    )

    private static func debugLog(_ message: String) {
        logger.debug("\(message, privacy: .public)")
        print("[WidgetSelectableEventsSyncService] \(message)")
        WidgetSharedDebugLog.append("[WidgetSelectableEventsSyncService] \(message)")
    }

    private let store: WidgetSelectableEventsStore

    init(store: WidgetSelectableEventsStore = .shared) {
        self.store = store
    }

    func add(event: WebEvent) throws -> WidgetSelectableEventAddResult {
        WidgetSharedDebugLog.clear()
        let exists = store.contains(eventID: event.id)
        let widgetEvent = try store.upsert(event: event)
        Self.debugLog(
            "add event id=\(widgetEvent.id) name=\(widgetEvent.name) cover=\(widgetEvent.coverImageURL ?? "nil") lineup=\(widgetEvent.lineupImageURL ?? "nil") preferred=\(widgetEvent.preferredBackgroundURL ?? "nil")"
        )

        if let preferredURL = widgetEvent.preferredBackgroundURL {
            Task {
                let relativePath = await WidgetBackgroundImageCache.fetchAndStore(
                    eventID: widgetEvent.id,
                    remoteURLString: preferredURL
                )

                if let relativePath {
                    let cachedEvent = WidgetSelectableEvent(
                        id: widgetEvent.id,
                        name: widgetEvent.name,
                        startDateISO8601: widgetEvent.startDateISO8601,
                        endDateISO8601: widgetEvent.endDateISO8601,
                        coverImageURL: widgetEvent.coverImageURL,
                        lineupImageURL: widgetEvent.lineupImageURL,
                        city: widgetEvent.city,
                        venueName: widgetEvent.venueName,
                        deeplinkURL: widgetEvent.deeplinkURL,
                        addedAtISO8601: widgetEvent.addedAtISO8601,
                        cachedBackgroundImageRelativePath: relativePath,
                        cachedBackgroundImageSourceURL: preferredURL
                    )
                    do {
                        try store.upsert(widgetEvent: cachedEvent)
                        Self.debugLog("cache metadata persisted event id=\(widgetEvent.id) relativePath=\(relativePath)")
                    } catch {
                        Self.debugLog("cache metadata persist failed event id=\(widgetEvent.id) error=\(error.localizedDescription)")
                    }
                }
                reloadWidgetsIfPossible()
            }
        }

        reloadWidgetsIfPossible()
        return exists ? .refreshed : .added
    }

    func remove(eventID: String) throws -> WidgetSelectableEventRemoveResult {
        let removedEvent = try store.remove(eventID: eventID)
        guard let removedEvent else {
            return .notFound
        }

        WidgetBackgroundImageCache.remove(relativePath: removedEvent.cachedBackgroundImageRelativePath)
        Self.debugLog("remove event id=\(removedEvent.id) relativePath=\(removedEvent.cachedBackgroundImageRelativePath ?? "nil")")
        reloadWidgetsIfPossible()
        return .removed
    }

    func contains(eventID: String) -> Bool {
        store.contains(eventID: eventID)
    }

    private func reloadWidgetsIfPossible() {
        #if canImport(WidgetKit)
        WidgetCenter.shared.reloadAllTimelines()
        #endif
    }
}

private struct EventSharePreviewCard: View {
    let payload: EventShareCardPayload

    var body: some View {
        HStack(alignment: .top, spacing: 12) {
            previewImage
                .frame(width: 72, height: 72)
                .clipShape(RoundedRectangle(cornerRadius: 12, style: .continuous))

            VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 6) {
                if let badge = payload.badgeText?.nilIfBlank {
                    Text(badge)
                        .font(.caption2.weight(.semibold))
                        .foregroundStyle(RaverTheme.accent)
                }

                Text(payload.eventName)
                    .font(.subheadline.weight(.semibold))
                    .foregroundStyle(RaverTheme.primaryText)
                    .lineLimit(2)

                if let venue = payload.venueName?.nilIfBlank {
                    Text(venue)
                        .font(.caption)
                        .foregroundStyle(RaverTheme.secondaryText)
                        .lineLimit(1)
                }
            }

            Spacer(minLength: 0)
        }
        .padding(12)
        .background(RaverTheme.card)
        .clipShape(RoundedRectangle(cornerRadius: 16, style: .continuous))
    }

    @ViewBuilder
    private var previewImage: some View {
        if let raw = payload.coverImageURL,
           let url = URL(string: raw),
           !raw.isEmpty {
            AsyncImage(url: url) { phase in
                switch phase {
                case .success(let image):
                    image.resizable().scaledToFill()
                default:
                    fallbackImage
                }
            }
        } else {
            fallbackImage
        }
    }

    private var fallbackImage: some View {
        LinearGradient(
            colors: [RaverTheme.accent.opacity(0.95), Color(red: 0.19, green: 0.18, blue: 0.26)],
            startPoint: .topLeading,
            endPoint: .bottomTrailing
        )
        .overlay(
            Image(systemName: "ticket.fill")
                .font(.system(size: 24, weight: .semibold))
                .foregroundStyle(Color.white.opacity(0.92))
        )
    }
}
